  ⚠ Bugs: Missing effect dependencies ×10
    Learn more: https://www.react.doctor/docs/rules/react-doctor/exhaustive-deps
    → Don't blindly add missing dependencies. Read the hook
    callback first.
    
    Bad:
    useEffect(() => {
      setCount(count + 1);
    }, [count]);
    
    Better:
    useEffect(() => {
      setCount((currentCount) => currentCount + 1);
    }, []);
    
    If the missing value is recreated every render, move it
    inside the hook or stabilize it before adding it to deps.

  ⚠ Bugs: Array index used as a key ×21
    Learn more: https://www.react.doctor/docs/rules/react-doctor/no-array-index-as-key
    → Use a stable id from the item, like `key={item.id}` or
    `key={item.slug}`. Index keys break when the list reorders
    or filters.

    Learn more: https://www.react.doctor/docs/rules/react-doctor/no-uncontrolled-input
    → Give `useState` a starting value (e.g. `useState("")`
    instead of `useState()`), add `onChange` (or `readOnly`)
    whenever you set `value`, and drop `defaultValue` on
    controlled inputs since React ignores it.

    Learn more: https://www.react.doctor/docs/rules/react-doctor/label-has-associated-control

    nesting the input.

    Learn more: https://www.react.doctor/docs/rules/react-doctor/no-mirror-prop-effect
    → Delete both the `useState` and the `useEffect` and read
    the prop directly while rendering. Copying a prop into

    effect catches up.

  ⚠ Performance: Non-passive scroll listener ×2
    Learn more: https://www.react.doctor/docs/rules/react-doctor/client-passive-event-listeners
    → Add `{ passive: true }` as the third argument:
    `addEventListener('scroll', handler, { passive: true })`.
    Only do this if the handler doesn't call
    `event.preventDefault()`, since passive listeners ignore it
    (which breaks pull-to-refresh, custom gestures, and nested
    scrolling).

  ⚠ Bugs: Effects chained together
    Learn more: https://www.react.doctor/docs/rules/react-doctor/no-effect-chain
    → Compute as much as possible during render (e.g. `const
    isGameOver = round > 5`) and write all related state inside
    the event handler that originally fires the chain. Each
    effect link adds an extra render and makes the code rigid
    as requirements evolve

  ⚠ Bugs: Effect re-subscribes on a changing callback ×5
    Learn more: https://www.react.doctor/docs/rules/react-doctor/prefer-use-effect-event
    → Wrap the callback with `useEffectEvent(callback)` (React
    19+) and call it inside the sub-handler. An Effect Event
    always sees the latest props and state but isn't a
    dependency, so the effect won't re-subscribe every time the
    parent redraws. See
    https://react.dev/reference/react/useEffectEvent

  ⚠ Bugs: Data passed to parent via effect ×4
    Learn more: https://www.react.doctor/docs/rules/react-doctor/no-pass-data-to-parent
    → Fetch the data in the parent and pass it down as a prop
    (or return it from the hook), instead of handing it back up
    through a prop callback in a useEffect. See
    https://react.dev/learn/you-might-not-need-an-effect#passing-data-to-the-parent

  ⚠ Maintainability: space-* utility on flex children ×10
    Learn more: https://www.react.doctor/docs/rules/react-doctor/design-no-space-on-flex-children
    → Use `gap-*` on the flex or grid parent. `space-x-*` and
    `space-y-*` leave gaps when a child is hidden, miss spacing
    on wrapped lines, and don't flip in right-to-left layouts.
